<div id="review_2622491231" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2622491231" />
    <a title="Maggie ☘" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/40477684-maggie"><img alt="Maggie ☘" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591529603p2/40477684.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2622491231?book_show_action=true">Dec 10, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maggie ☘" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maggie ☘" href="/user/show/40477684-maggie">Maggie ☘</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/40477684-maggie?shelf=contemporary-na">contemporary-na</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/40477684-maggie?shelf=unpopular-opinions">unpopular-opinions</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2622491231" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9229841165693606182">*3.5/5 stars*<br/><br/>This book was light and fun read for me, I really enjoyed the budding friendship between Emily, Dawn, Collins and Frank. I also liked how Emily slowly came out of her shell. The List was such an entertaining idea, and the playlists included were a cherry on top (Frank's music taste all the way btw!) Her family, especially Emily's younger brother Beckett, were amazing! Collins was also such a fun character.<br/><br/>The reasons as to why I didn't give it 4 stars in the end were 1. I didn't enj</span>
  <span id="freeText9229841165693606182" style="display:none">*3.5/5 stars*<br /><br />This book was light and fun read for me, I really enjoyed the budding friendship between Emily, Dawn, Collins and Frank. I also liked how Emily slowly came out of her shell. The List was such an entertaining idea, and the playlists included were a cherry on top (Frank's music taste all the way btw!) Her family, especially Emily's younger brother Beckett, were amazing! Collins was also such a fun character.<br /><br />The reasons as to why I didn't give it 4 stars in the end were 1. I didn't enjoy the last sequence of the book as much and the ending didn't show us what happened with <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Emily and Dawn's friendship, nor Emily and Collins's. Of course I assume she will be friends with Collins because he is Frank's best friend, but Dawn was really upset and I just don't get how a frienship/s that were bult through the book could be left this way when it is what this book was about. We get wrepped up romance ending but not the female frienship I rooted for more, why??? <br /><br />I wished this book ended up with all of them together, not just Emily and Frank, as the romance wasn't the most important relationship of this book, the new friendships were. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br />2. As much as I liked the love interest as a character, as much as I liked his friendship with Emily and the band, I couldn't entirely ship the situation <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[the fact that he had a long term girlfriend the whole way through, breaking up with her just at the end. I mean, the situation was done, well, not badly, and Emily never once antagonized her as (ehm ehm Anna in Anna and the French Kiss did.. ugh that book!) but as much as I liked them as a friends... because of this, I wished this book didn't have any romance or that he broke up with Lissa at the beggining of the novel rather than the end. It would've also been less drama, which was the last sequence I didn't enjoy as much anyway. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />I was undecided about Sloane the whole way through this book honestly. Through a lot of this book, she was this idea for us reader told from Emily's view, sometimes appearing in short flashbacks. I liked that it was a flawed friendship, but nonetheless important and at some point all encompassing to Emily. It was interesting, how given some time apart from Sloane, Emily ultimately grew a voice entirely of her own <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[but still was friends with Sloane in the end. Just a bit different friend. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I loved that this book showed us just how important and defining friendship can be to a lot of young girls. I also liked that the friendship between Emily and Sloane had its good and bad side, especially as they were such a starkly diffeent characters, sometimes they benefitted from each other, other times they didn't entirely fit. And sometimes I couldn't help but think Sloane wasn't the best of friends, plus a manic pixie dream girl (at the beginning especially), other times I got why she was written this way. But I think the ending convinced me to be more on her side then I may have been before, plus I love that at its heart this book is about their friendship.<br /><br />All in all, the thing I enjoyed most about this book were the various friendships, and how light, fun read it was. I will definitely pick up other books by this author. </span>
  <a data-text-id="9229841165693606182" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1294775143" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1294775143" />
    <a title="Anja H." class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6054186-anja-h"><img alt="Anja H." src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1559051853p2/6054186.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1294775143?book_show_action=true">May 31, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anja H." class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anja H." href="/user/show/6054186-anja-h">Anja H.</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1294775143" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7113801988672647423"><b>*5 SUMMERY STARS*</b><br/><br/>This book is such a perfect summer read! <br/>Even though it's currently raining outside here, this book really made me feel happy and wanting to go on adventures and meet new people!<br/><i>Since You've Been Gone</i> is about Emily, who wakes up one day, discovering that her best friend is gone but she left her a list of things to do. In the process of doing that, Emily makes new friends, falls in love, finds herself and figures out why her best friend left and where she went.<br/>This book isn't th</span>
  <span id="freeText7113801988672647423" style="display:none"><b>*5 SUMMERY STARS*</b><br /><br />This book is such a perfect summer read! <br />Even though it's currently raining outside here, this book really made me feel happy and wanting to go on adventures and meet new people!<br /><i>Since You've Been Gone</i> is about Emily, who wakes up one day, discovering that her best friend is gone but she left her a list of things to do. In the process of doing that, Emily makes new friends, falls in love, finds herself and figures out why her best friend left and where she went.<br />This book isn't the most original story out there, in fact it kinda reminds me of <i>Paper Towns</i> (only I liked this ending way better! This book is the one that made me retract 1 star off my previously-5-star Paper Towns rating btw), and it was a little predictable at times, but it was just so well executed and thought out that I'm giving this 5 stars anyway!<br />I loved seeing Emily evolve from an introverted girl to someone who could make choices for herself and dares to speak up. It kind of reminded me of myself a bit and about how I used to be.<br />I secretly dislike Sloane a bit though. During the flashbacks, I didn't like the power that Sloane sometimes had over Emily. Their friendship just didn't seem all that healthy to me. It's definitely good that Emily grew a backbone in the end! The person I dislike the most is Sam though, no worries!<br />The story was a bit slow at times, but as soon as Frank started helping her on the list, things definitely picked up! I love that there wasn't any kind of insta-love here and you really saw their relationship grow.<br />Overall, I really loved this and I advise anyone who hasn't read this yet, to definitely pick this one up <u>asap</u>!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7113801988672647423" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('SBnUfgcEWaxthG1fzPIQ9Poum1dWmWykQI/Rw2wz4UgJRWJu+n4x7r+ycArIQFy/qZzkZEH6Gf4WR94hyH5tFA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('x2DaY60D63aKB2+v/I9SGRmxdv83odFpX0k/LTj+/AKGPGxzUHmDNFgxcvr4PR5SSgMJzCDCpDMJgTDPnLNwXg==')})
  }

      <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/3351454.Morgan_Matson">About Morgan Matson</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/3351454.Morgan_Matson"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1281591801p3/3351454.jpg);'></div>
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__widgetContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__name'>
<a href="/author/show/3351454.Morgan_Matson">Morgan Matson
</a></div>
<div class='goodreadsAuthorBadge'></div>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer14530884400862567747">Morgan Matson grew up in New York City and Greenwich, Connecticut. She attended Occidental College in Los Angeles but halfway though a theater degree, she started working in the children's department of Vroman's Bookstore and fell in love with YA literature.<br/><br/>Following college graduation (and the proud bearer of an incredibly useful theater/English degree) she moved back East to attend the New Schoo</span>
  <span id="freeText14530884400862567747" style="display:none">Morgan Matson grew up in New York City and Greenwich, Connecticut. She attended Occidental College in Los Angeles but halfway though a theater degree, she started working in the children's department of Vroman's Bookstore and fell in love with YA literature.<br /><br />Following college graduation (and the proud bearer of an incredibly useful theater/English degree) she moved back East to attend the New School, where she received her M.F.A in Writing for Children.<br /><br />Amy &amp; Roger's Epic Detour, inspired by Morgan's three cross-country road trips, was published in May 2010. It was named an ALA Top Ten Best Book, a PW "Flying Start" book, and was shortlisted for the Waterstone's Book Prize.<br /><br />In the meantime, Morgan moved back to California, went back to school again and in 2011 received an M.F.A. in Screenwriting from the University of Southern California.<br /><br />Her second book, Second Chance Summer, was published in May 2012 and draws largely on her experiences spending summers growing up in the Pocono Mountains of Pennsylvania.<br /><br />Her third book, Since You've Been Gone, was published in 2014. <br /><br />Morgan currently lives in Los Angeles, though she loves to travel and does it whenever she can. She is currently writing another book, to be published in 2016.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14530884400862567747" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
